add_namespace = rw_germany

#Risen from the Ruin
country_event = {
	id = rw_germany.1
	title = rw_germany.1.t
	desc = rw_germany.1.d
	picture = risen_from_the_ruin

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rw_germany.1.o1
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				days = 2
				id = rw_germany.2
			}
			country_event = {
				days = 4
				id = rw_germany.3
			}
			country_event = {
				days = 6
				id = rw_germany.4
			}
		}
	}
}

#Drug policy proposed
country_event = {
	id = rw_germany.6
	title = rw_germany.6.t
	desc = rw_germany.6.d
	picture = progressives_propose_drug_bill

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Support it
		name = rw_germany.6.o1
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_MODROW
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_MERKEL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_GYSI
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_progressive_narcotics_bill
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_germany.11
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Dismiss it
		name = rw_germany.6.o2
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_KRENZ
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_WAGENKNECHT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_JAHN
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_germany.7
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
}

#Progressives Revolt
country_event = {
	id = rw_germany.7
	title = rw_germany.7.t
	desc = rw_germany.7.d
	picture = progressives_outraged

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Backtrack
		name = rw_germany.7.o1
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_MODROW
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_MERKEL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_GYSI
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_progressive_narcotics_bill
		add_political_power = -100
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_germany.11
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Continue
		name = rw_germany.7.o2
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_KRENZ
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_WAGENKNECHT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_JAHN
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_germany.8
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
}

			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis

					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_MERKEL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_GYSI
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_progressive_narcotics_bill
		add_political_power = -200
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_germany.11
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Continue
		name = rw_germany.9.o2
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_KRENZ
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_WAGENKNECHT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_JAHN
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_germany.10
				days = 3
			}
		}
		GER_volkskammer = {
			promote_character = leninist
		}
	}
}

#Krenz becomes Premier
country_event = {
	id = rw_germany.10
	title = rw_germany.10.t
	desc = rw_germany.10.d
	picture = krenz_becomes_premier

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Cool
		name = rw_germany.10.o1
		set_country_flag = GER_krenz_coup
		set_country_flag = GER_hardliners_in_power
		GER_egon_krenz = {
			promote_character = stalinist
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_hardline_cabinet_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = germany_ind_gunther_kleiber
			add_ideas = germany_nsm_sahra_wagenknecht
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					hours = 4
					id = rw_germany_news.17
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Should Krenz retire?
country_event = {
	id = rw_germany.21
	title = rw_germany.21.t
	desc = rw_germany.21.d
	picture = krenz_resign

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Leggo my Ego(n)
		name = rw_germany.21.o1
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_KRENZ
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_the_general_secretarys_solution }
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		set_country_flag = GER_congress_krenz
	}
	
	option = { #Retire
		name = rw_germany.21.o2
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_WAGENKNECHT
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = GER_the_general_secretarys_solution }
			set_country_flag = GER_congress_jahn
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = GER_congress_wagenknecht
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
	}
}

#Jahn becomes Premier
country_event = {
	id = rw_germany.22
	title = rw_germany.22.t
	desc = rw_germany.22.d
	picture = sed_congress

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Egon Krenz"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_country_flag = GER_congress_jahn
	}
	
	option = { #Long live the Premier
		name = rw_germany.22.o1
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		GER_sigmund_jahn = {
			promote_character = stalinist
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_congress_concluded
		remove_ideas = germany_sic_sigmund_jahn
		add_ideas = germany_sic_margot_honecker
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					hours = 4
					id = rw_germany_news.24
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#SED Congress
country_event = {
	id = rw_germany.32
	title = rw_germany.32.t
	desc = rw_germany.32.d
	picture = sed_congress

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Hans Modrow"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Nothing ever happens
		name = rw_germany.32.o1
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_MODROW
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_germany.33
				days = 4
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Modroever
		name = rw_germany.32.o2
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_MERKEL
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_opioid_crisis
						option = GER_OPIOID_CRISIS_GYSI
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = germany_sic_angela_merkel }
				country_event = {
					id = rw_germany.34
					days = 4
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = germany_sic_gregor_gysi }
				country_event = {
					id = rw_germany.35
					days = 4
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Party of Democratic Socialism
country_event = {
	id = rw_germany.94
	title = rw_germany.94.t
	desc = rw_germany.94.d
	picture = gysi_democratic_socialism

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #
		name = rw_germany.94.o1
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = moderate_socialist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
	}
	
	option = { #
		name = rw_germany.94.o2
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { GER_gysi_progressive > 3 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_sed_will_switch_to_modsoc
		set_party_name = {
			name = GER_sed_modsoc_party
			long_name = GER_sed_modsoc_party_long
			ideology = moderate_socialist
		}
		set_party_name = {
			name = GER_sed_hardliners_party
			long_name = GER_sed_hardliners_party_long
			ideology = communist
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = moderate_socialist 
			popularity = 0.12
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { name = "Gregor Gysi" ruling_only = yes } }
				GER_gregor_gysi = {
					add_country_leader_role = {
						country_leader = {
							expire = "1.1.1.1"
							desc = "POLITICS_GER_GREGOR_GYSI_DESC"
							ideology = peoples_socialist_democracy
							traits = { GER_grotewohl_not_ulbricht }
						}
					}
					promote_character = peoples_socialist_democracy
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = communist }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = moderate_socialist
				}
				set_variable = {
					current_modsoc_pop = party_popularity@moderate_socialist
				}
				set_variable = {
					current_commie_pop = party_popularity@communist
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = current_commie_pop
					value = current_modsoc_pop
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = moderate_socialist
					popularity = current_commie_pop
				}	
				add_communist_to_coalition = yes
				add_nationalist_to_coalition = yes
				add_natcon_to_coalition = yes
				add_centrist_to_coalition = yes
				add_liberal_to_coalition = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = EUU } }
				set_cosmetic_tag = GER_ddr_real
			}
			GER_sahra_wagenknecht = {
				promote_character = stalinist
			}
		}
	}
}

#Stasi Coup
country_event = {
	id = rw_germany.100
	title = rw_germany.100.t
	desc = rw_germany.100.d
	picture = gysi_smoking

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #
		name = rw_germany.100.o1
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = national_bolshevik
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_bolshevik
			popularity = 0.3
		}
		every_country = {
			news_event = {
				hours = 4
				id = rw_germany_news.25
			}
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = GER_ddr_real
		set_country_flag = GER_democratization_reversed
		clr_country_flag = GER_moderates_in_power
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = GER_shit_is_going_down }
			country_event = {
				id = rw_ger_monarchist.1
				days = 6
			}
		}
		else = {
			clr_country_flag = GER_time_of_change
			set_country_flag = GER_stasi_coup_flag
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			add_ideas = GER_remains_of_resistance
			add_ideas = GER_legacy_of_the_coup
			add_ideas = GER_counter_culture_movement
			remove_ideas = GER_national_front2_gysi
			remove_ideas = GER_demise_of_the_hardliners
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_wolf_legacy3
				add_idea = GER_wolf_legacy
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_westalgie2
				add_idea = GER_westalgie
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = GER_shield_and_sword_gysi2 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_shield_and_sword_gysi2
					add_idea = GER_shield_and_sword
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = GER_shield_and_sword_gysi3 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_shield_and_sword_gysi3
					add_idea = GER_shield_and_sword
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = GER_shield_and_sword_gysi4 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_shield_and_sword_gysi4
					add_idea = GER_shield_and_sword
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Pre-Party Congress (Gysi)
country_event = {
	id = rw_germany.101
	title = rw_germany.101.t
	desc = rw_germany.101.d
	picture = preparing_for_17th_congress

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #We're Progressive
		name = rw_germany.101.o1
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_gysi_conservative > 3 }
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						id = rw_germany.103
						days = 4
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = rw_germany.104
					days = 4
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #We're Moderate actually
		name = rw_germany.101.o2
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = moderate_socialist }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_gysi_progressive > 3 }
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = {
						id = rw_germany.102
						days = 4
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = rw_germany.104
					days = 4
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

			add_country_leader_role = {
				country_leader = {
					expire = "1.1.1.1"

				}
			}
			promote_character = goulash_communist
		}
		GER_bodo_ramelow = {
			promote_character = european_moderate_socialist
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_next_congress_concluded
	}
}

#Next Congress Trigger
country_event = {
	id = rw_germany.188
	title = rw_germany.188.t
	desc = rw_germany.188.d
	picture = preparing_for_17th_congress
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_leader = { character = GER_hans_modrow ruling_only = yes }
			}
			country_event = rw_germany.126
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_leader = { character = GER_angela_merkel ruling_only = yes }
			}
			country_event = rw_germany.139
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_leader = { character = GER_sigmund_jahn ruling_only = yes }
			}
			country_event = rw_germany.161
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_leader = { character = GER_gregor_gysi ruling_only = yes }
			}
			country_event = rw_germany.101
		}
		else = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_germany.150
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	
	hidden = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		GER_is_ddr = yes
	}
	
	option = { #
		name = rw_germany.188.o1
		
	}
}

#WE ARE OUT OF GAS 
country_event = {
	id = rw_germany.218
	title = rw_germany.218.t
	desc = {
		text = rw_germany.218.d_3
		trigger = {
			SOV = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = communist
					has_government = revolutionary_socialist
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_germany.218.d_2
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = SOV }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_germany.218.d
	}
	
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		OR = {
			has_war_with = RUS
			has_war_with = SOV
		}
	}
	
	picture = russian_oil_cut_off

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #
		name = rw_germany.218.o1
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = IRQ }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea4 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea4
				add_idea = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea_bad4
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea3 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea3
				add_idea = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea_bad3
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea2
				add_idea = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea_bad2
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea
				add_idea = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea_bad
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea_less }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea_less
				add_idea = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea_bad_less
			}
		}
		
		uncomplete_national_focus = {
			focus = GER_reliance_on_russian_gas
			uncomplete_children = no
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_cut_off_from_russian_fuel
	}
	
	option = { #
		name = rw_germany.218.o1
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = IRQ 
		}
		remove_ideas = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea4
		remove_ideas = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea3
		remove_ideas = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea2
		remove_ideas = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea
		remove_ideas = GER_russian_gas_reliance_idea_less
		uncomplete_national_focus = {
			focus = GER_reliance_on_russian_gas
			uncomplete_children = no
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_cut_off_from_russian_fuel
	}
}

#Gunther Shabowsky Death
country_event = {
	id = rw_germany.220
	title = rw_germany.220.t
	desc = rw_germany.220.d
	picture = shabowsky_death

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		GER_is_ddr = yes 
	}
	
	option = { #
		name = rw_germany.220.o1
		add_manpower = -1
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { 
					OR = {
						has_government = moderate_socialist
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Gregor Gysi"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			GER_wolfgang_berghofer = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader={
						ideology=peoples_socialist_democracy
						expire="1.1.1.1"
						id=-1
					}
				}
				promote_character = peoples_socialist_democracy
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_schabowsky_dead
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = germany_nsm_gunter_schabowski }
			remove_ideas = germany_nsm_gunter_schabowski
			add_ideas = germany_nsm_bernd_riexinger
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = germany_sic_gunter_schabowski }
			remove_ideas = germany_sic_gunter_schabowski
			add_ideas = germany_sic_klaus_schwab
		}
	}
}

add_namespace = rw_ger_democratic

#Provisional Govt
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_democratic.1
	title = rw_ger_democratic.1.t
	desc = rw_ger_democratic.1.d
	picture = provisional_government_formed

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rw_ger_democratic.1.o1
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communist
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		GER_set_tree_visibility = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			64 = {
				set_province_name = {
					id = 9496
					name = "Eisenhüttenstadt"
				}
			}
			66 = {
				set_province_name = {
					id = 9471
					name = "Chemnitz"
				}
			}
			56 = {
				set_province_name = {
					id = 241
					name = "Wilhelmshaven"
				}
			}
			42 = {
				set_province_name = {
					id = 3558
					name = "Kaiserslautern"
				}
			}
			50 = {
				set_province_name = {
					id = 6934
					name = "Friedrichshafen"
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = GER_reanamed_karl_marx_stadt }
				42 = {
					set_province_name = {
						id = 9575
						name = "Trier"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Lander restored
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_democratic.3
	title = rw_ger_democratic.3.t
	desc = rw_ger_democratic.3.d
	picture = restoration_of_the_states

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rw_ger_democratic.3.o1
		add_stability = 0.02
		set_country_flag = GER_localist
		add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = 0.04 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = centrist popularity = 0.04 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = national_conservative popularity = 0.04 }
	}
	option = {
		name = rw_ger_democratic.3.o2
		add_political_power = 20
		set_country_flag = GER_centralized
		add_popularity = { ideology = moderate_socialist popularity = 0.04 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = liberal popularity = 0.04 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = communist popularity = 0.04 }
	}
}

#Outcome of the Trials
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_democratic.9
	title = rw_ger_democratic.9.t
	desc = {
		text= rw_ger_democratic.9.d_harsh
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { GER_sed_jail > GER_sed_free }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text= rw_ger_democratic.9.d_equal
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { GER_sed_jail = GER_sed_free }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text= rw_ger_democratic.9.d_lenient
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { GER_sed_jail < GER_sed_free }
		}
	}
	picture = end_of_the_trials

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rw_ger_democratic.9.o1
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_sed_jail > GER_sed_free }
			}
			add_political_power = 50
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communist
				popularity = -0.04
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = moderate_socialist
				popularity = -0.02
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_sed_jail = GER_sed_free }
			}
			add_political_power = -25
			add_stability = 0.02
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = moderate_socialist
				popularity = 0.04
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -50
			add_stability = 0.05
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communist
				popularity = 0.04
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = moderate_socialist
				popularity = 0.08
			}
		}
	}
}

#SED-PDS Formed
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_democratic.17
	title = rw_ger_democratic.17.t
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_democratic.17.d_gysi
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_gysi_is_in_prison } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_democratic.17.d_other
		trigger = { has_country_flag = GER_gysi_is_in_prison }
	}
	picture = sed_pds_founded

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rw_ger_democratic.17.o1
		GER_kate_niederkirchner = {
			promote_character = moderate_socialist_ideology
		}
		set_party_name = {
			name = GER_sed_pds_party
			long_name = GER_sed_pds_party_long
			ideology = moderate_socialist
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rw_ger_democratic.17.o2
		GER_olaf_scholz = {
			promote_character = moderate_socialist_ideology
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_firstround_scholz
		set_party_name = {
			name = GER_sed_pds_party
			long_name = GER_sed_pds_party_long
			ideology = moderate_socialist
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rw_ger_democratic.17.o3
		GER_gerhard_schroeder = {
			promote_character = moderate_socialist_ideology
		}
		set_party_name = {
			name = GER_sed_pds_party
			long_name = GER_sed_pds_party_long
			ideology = moderate_socialist
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rw_ger_democratic.17.o4
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_gysi_is_in_prison }
		}
		GER_gregor_gysi = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
				country_leader = {
					expire = "1.1.1.1"
					ideology = moderate_socialist_ideology
				}
			}
			promote_character = moderate_socialist_ideology
		}
		set_party_name = {
			name = GER_sed_pds_party
			long_name = GER_sed_pds_party_long
			ideology = moderate_socialist
		}
	}
}

#Election
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_democratic.24
	title = rw_ger_democratic.24.t
	desc = rw_ger_democratic.24.d
	picture = germany_election

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { GER_sed_pds_win = 0 }
			set_variable = { GER_spd_win = 0 }
			set_variable = { GER_ldpd_win = 0 }
			set_variable = { GER_dbd_win = 0 }
			set_variable = { GER_cdu_win = 0 }
			set_variable = { GER_ndpd_win = 0 }
		}
	}
	
	option = { #SED-PDS
		name = rw_ger_democratic.24.o1
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_democratic
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_democratic
						option = GER_DEMOCRATIC_SED_PDS
					}					
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}		
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = moderate_socialist
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = moderate_socialist
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		country_event = rw_ger_democratic.25
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_sed_pds_cabinet_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = {
				germany_sic_bodo_ramelow
				germany_fom_katja_kipping
				germany_ind_oskar_lafontaine
				germany_nsm_dietmar_bartsch
			}
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					hours = 4
					id = rw_germany_news.16
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_elections_finished
		add_to_variable = { GER_sed_pds_win = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { #Next Election
				id = rw_ger_democratic.57
				days = 1463
			}
			country_event = { #SPD Leadership
				id = rw_ger_democratic.52
				days = 1350
			}
			country_event = { #LDPD Leadership
				id = rw_ger_democratic.53
				days = 1300
			}
			country_event = { #DBD Leadership
				id = rw_ger_democratic.54
				days = 1250
			}
			country_event = { #CDU Leadership
				id = rw_ger_democratic.55
				days = 1200
			}
			country_event = { #NDPD Leadership
				id = rw_ger_democratic.56
				days = 1150
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #SPD
		name = rw_ger_democratic.24.o2
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_democratic
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_democratic
						option = GER_DEMOCRATIC_SPD
					}					
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = new_democrat
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = new_democrat
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		country_event = rw_ger_democratic.25
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_sdp_cabinet_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = {
				germany_sic_franz_muntefering
				germany_fom_markus_meckel
				germany_ind_hubertus_heil
				germany_nsm_karl_lauterbach
			}
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					hours = 4
					id = rw_germany_news.15
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_elections_finished
		add_to_variable = { GER_spd_win = 1 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { #Next Election
				id = rw_ger_democratic.57
				days = 1463
			}
			country_event = { #SED-PDS Leadership
				id = rw_ger_democratic.51
				days = 1350
			}
			country_event = { #LDPD Leadership
				id = rw_ger_democratic.53

#Coalition
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_democratic.25
	title = rw_ger_democratic.25.t
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_democratic.25.d_sed
		trigger = { has_government = moderate_socialist }
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_democratic.25.d_spd
		trigger = { has_government = new_democrat }
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_democratic.25.d_ldpd
		trigger = { has_government = liberal }
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_democratic.25.d_dbd
		trigger = { has_government = centrist }
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_democratic.25.d_cdu
		trigger = { has_government = national_conservative }
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_democratic.25.d_ndpd
		trigger = { has_government = nationalist }
	}
	picture = bundestag_legislative_coalition
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = GER_shut_out_of_the_legislature
			remove_ideas = GER_shut_out_of_the_legislature2
			remove_ideas = GER_shut_out_of_the_legislature3
			remove_ideas = GER_romania_coalition
			remove_ideas = GER_grand_coalition
			remove_ideas = GER_traffic_light_coalition
			remove_ideas = GER_gambia_coalition
			remove_ideas = GER_countryside_coalition
			remove_ideas = GER_ukraine_coalition
			remove_ideas = GER_new_caledonia_coalition
			remove_ideas = GER_social_liberal_coalition
			remove_ideas = GER_red_green_coalition
			end_coalition = yes
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #SED-PDS/NDPD (Coalitions Locked)
		trigger = {
			OR = { 
				has_government = nationalist
				has_government = moderate_socialist
			}
		}
		name = rw_ger_democratic.25.o1
		add_stability = -0.05
		CAN_subtract_3_percent_popularity = yes
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_firewall_idea_2 } }
			add_ideas = GER_shut_out_of_the_legislature
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = GER_firewall_idea_2 }
			add_ideas = GER_shut_out_of_the_legislature2
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = GER_shut_out_of_the_legislature3
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Romania Coalition - LDPD/CDU/SPD
		trigger = {
			OR = { 
				has_government = new_democrat
				has_government = liberal
				has_government = national_conservative
			}
		}
		name = rw_ger_democratic.25.o2
		add_ideas = GER_romania_coalition
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = new_democrat } }
			add_newdem_to_coalition = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = liberal } }
			add_liberal_to_coalition = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = national_conservative } }
			add_natcon_to_coalition = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Grand Coalition - CDU/SPD
		trigger = {
			OR = { 
				has_government = new_democrat
				has_government = national_conservative
			}
		}
		name = rw_ger_democratic.25.o3
		add_ideas = GER_grand_coalition
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = new_democrat } }
			add_newdem_to_coalition = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = national_conservative } }
			add_natcon_to_coalition = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Traffic Light - DBD/SPD/LDPD
		trigger = {
			OR = {

				has_government = liberal
				has_government = centrist
			}

	id = rw_ger_democratic.73

	desc = rw_ger_democratic.73.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

add_namespace = rw_ger_monarchist

#Things go to shit
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_monarchist.1
	title = rw_ger_monarchist.1.t
	desc = rw_ger_monarchist.1.d
	picture = kujat_takes_over

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rw_ger_monarchist.1.o1
		set_party_name = {
			long_name = GER_military_coup_party_long
			name = GER_military_coup_party
			ideology = nationalist
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = nationalist
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = nationalist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		GER_harald_kujat = {
			promote_character = military_junta
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = GER_prov_gov
		set_country_flag = GER_military_coup_occured
		create_dynamic_country = {	#Stasi Coup
			original_tag = GER
			copy_tag = GER
			
			save_global_event_target_as = stasi_civil_war_target

			### Politics
			set_popularities = {
				fascist = 5
				nationalist = 0
				monarchist = 0
				national_bolshevik = 75
				national_conservative = 0
				centrist = 0
				liberal = 0
				new_democrat = 0
				moderate_socialist = 0
				revolutionary_socialist = 0
				communist = 20
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_bolshevik
				long_name = GER_stasi_party_long
				name = GER_stasi_party
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = national_bolshevik
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = GER_STASI_GOVT
		}
		GER_wolfgang_schwanitz = {
			set_nationality = event_target:stasi_civil_war_target
		}
		event_target:stasi_civil_war_target = { 
			GER_wolfgang_schwanitz = {
				promote_character = securocracy
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader={
						ideology=securocracy
						expire="1.1.1.1"
						traits = { GER_cornered_rat }
						id=-1
					}
				}
				promote_character = securocracy
				add_trait = {
					trait = GER_cornered_rat
					ideology = securocracy 
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { 
				is_in_west_germany = no
				NOT = { is_core_of = AUS }
			}
			event_target:stasi_civil_war_target = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		event_target:stasi_civil_war_target = {
			division_template = {
				name = "Felix Dzerzhinsky Guards Regiment"
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				}
			}
			
			every_owned_state = {
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Stasi Division\" division_template = \"Felix Dzerzhinsky Guards Regiment\" start_experience_factor = 0.5" 
					owner = PREV
				}
				
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Stasi Division\" division_template = \"Felix Dzerzhinsky Guards Regiment\" start_experience_factor = 0.5" 
					owner = PREV
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Stasi Division\" division_template = \"Felix Dzerzhinsky Guards Regiment\" start_experience_factor = 0.5" 
					owner = PREV
				}
				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Stasi Division\" division_template = \"Felix Dzerzhinsky Guards Regiment\" start_experience_factor = 0.5" 
					owner = PREV
				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {

				create_unit = { 
					division = "name = \"Stasi Division\" division_template = \"Felix Dzerzhinsky Guards Regiment\" start_experience_factor = 0.5" 
					owner = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_trait = GER_nva_officer_trait }
			set_nationality = event_target:stasi_civil_war_target
		}
		transfer_units_fraction = {
			target = event_target:stasi_civil_war_target
			size = 0.25
			army_ratio = 0.25
			navy_ratio = 0.25
			air_ratio = 0.25
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
			FRA = { set_faction_leader = yes }
			set_global_flag = FRA_is_faction_leader
		}
		leave_faction = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_ger_monarchist.2
				days = 5
			}
			if = {
				limit = { ITA = { is_in_faction_with = FRA } }
				ITA = {
					country_event = rw_ger_democratic_diplo.2
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				country_event = rw_ger_democratic_diplo.2
			}
			BEL = {
				country_event = rw_ger_democratic_diplo.2
			}
			LUX = {
				country_event = rw_ger_democratic_diplo.2
			}
			HOL = {
				country_event = rw_ger_democratic_diplo.2
			}
		}
		
		remove_ideas = idea_eu_member
		remove_ideas = idea_comecon_member
		set_country_flag = GER_junta_in_power
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = germany_sic_wolfgang_schneiderhan
			add_ideas = germany_for_carsten_breuer
			add_ideas = germany_inm_eberhard_zorn
			add_ideas = germany_nsm_jorg_vollmer
		}
		create_intelligence_agency = {
			name = "Militärischer Abschirmdienst"
			icon = GFX_intelligence_agency_logo_ger_democratic_alt
		}
		GER_set_tree_visibility = yes
		remove_opinion_modifier = {
			target = CAN
			modifier = denounced_warsaw_pact
		}
		CAN = {
			remove_opinion_modifier = {
				target = GER
				modifier = denounced_warsaw_pact
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = CAN_democratic_support_surge
		remove_ideas = CAN_chaos_in_the_warsaw_pact
		remove_ideas = CAN_bad_intel_idea
		remove_ideas = CAN_bad_intel_idea_lar
		remove_ideas = GER_empowered_democratic_resistance
		remove_ideas = CAN_canadian_sabatoge
		56 = {
			set_province_name = {
				id = 241
				name = "Wilhelmshaven"
			}
		}
		42 = {
			set_province_name = {
				id = 3558
				name = "Kaiserslautern"
			}
		}
		50 = {
			set_province_name = {
				id = 6934
				name = "Friedrichshafen"
			}
		}
	}
}

#Austria Nopes Out
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_monarchist.2
	title = rw_ger_monarchist.2.t
	desc = rw_ger_monarchist.2.d
	picture = kurz_emerges

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rw_ger_monarchist.2.o1
		release = AUS
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_trait = GER_bundesheer_officer_trait }
			set_nationality = AUS
		}
		remove_ideas = GER_austrian_unhappiness
	}
}

#Civil War Begins
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_monarchist.3
	title = rw_ger_monarchist.3.t
	desc = rw_ger_monarchist.3.d
	picture = civil_war_in_germany

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rw_ger_monarchist.3.o1
		declare_war_on = {
			target = var:64.owner
			type = annex_everything
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communist
			popularity = -0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = nationalist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_civil_war_has_begun
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				news_event = {
					hours = 4
					id = rw_germany_news.2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Repay the Prince of Reuss?
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_monarchist.16
	title = rw_ger_monarchist.16.t
	desc = rw_ger_monarchist.16.d
	picture = reward_the_prince_of_reuss

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = rw_ger_monarchist.16.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = GER_monarchist
							option = DEFAULT
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = GER_monarchist
							option = GER_MONARCHIST_ABSOLUTE
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = GER_monarchist
							option = GER_MONARCHIST_REICHBURGER
						}				
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_reuss_in_power
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_reuss_warning_tt
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rw_ger_monarchist.16.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_monarchist
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_monarchist
						option = GER_MONARCHIST_ABSOLUTE
					}
					AND = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = GER_monarchist
							option = GER_MONARCHIST_REICHBURGER
						}					
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascist
			popularity = -0.02
		}
	}
}

		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_frederick_iv_tooltip

			popularity = 0.02

	}
	
	option = {

#Coalition
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_monarchist.28
	title = rw_ger_monarchist.28.t
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_monarchist.28.d_uspd
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				has_government = moderate_socialist 
				AND = {
					has_government = monarchist 
					has_country_flag = GER_uspd_in_power
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_monarchist.28.d_spd
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				has_government = new_democrat 
				AND = {
					has_government = monarchist 
					has_country_flag = GER_spd_in_power
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_monarchist.28.d_fvp
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				has_government = liberal 
				AND = {
					has_government = monarchist 
					has_country_flag = GER_fvp_in_power
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_monarchist.28.d_nlp
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				has_government = centrist
				AND = {
					has_government = monarchist 
					has_country_flag = GER_nlp_in_power
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_monarchist.28.d_cdu
		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				has_government = national_conservative 
				AND = {
					has_government = monarchist 
					has_country_flag = GER_cdu_zentrum_in_power
				}
			}
		}
	}
	picture = bundestag_legislative_coalition
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = GER_romania_coalition_monarchist
			remove_ideas = GER_grand_coalition_monarchist
			remove_ideas = GER_traffic_light_coalition_monarchist
			remove_ideas = GER_gambia_coalition_monarchist
			remove_ideas = GER_burgerbloc_coalition
			remove_ideas = GER_ukraine_coalition_monarchist
			remove_ideas = GER_new_caledonia_coalition_monarchist
			remove_ideas = GER_social_liberal_coalition_fvp_monarchist
			remove_ideas = GER_social_liberal_coalition_nlp_monarchist
			remove_ideas = GER_red_red_coalition_monarchist
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_kaiser_in_command }
				}
				end_coalition = yes
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Grand Coalition - CDU/SPD
		trigger = {
			OR = { 
				OR = {
					has_government = new_democrat
					AND = {
						has_government = monarchist 
						has_country_flag = GER_spd_in_power
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_government = national_conservative
					AND = {
						has_government = monarchist 
						has_country_flag = GER_cdu_zentrum_in_power
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = rw_ger_monarchist.28.o1
		add_ideas = GER_grand_coalition_monarchist
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = new_democrat } }
			add_newdem_to_coalition = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = national_conservative } }
			add_natcon_to_coalition = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Romania Coalition - FVP/CDU/SPD
		trigger = {
			OR = { 
				OR = {
					has_government = new_democrat
					AND = {
						has_government = monarchist 
						has_country_flag = GER_spd_in_power
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_government = liberal
					AND = {
						has_government = monarchist 
						has_country_flag = GER_fvp_in_power
					}
				}
				OR = {
					has_government = national_conservative
					AND = {
						has_government = monarchist 
						has_country_flag = GER_cdu_zentrum_in_power
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = rw_ger_monarchist.28.o2
		add_ideas = GER_romania_coalition_monarchist
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = new_democrat } }
			add_newdem_to_coalition = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = liberal } }
			add_liberal_to_coalition = yes
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_government = national_conservative } }
			add_natcon_to_coalition = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Traffic Light - FVP/SPD/NLP
		trigger = {
			OR = { 
				OR = {
					has_government = new_democrat
					AND = {

#Election 2
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_monarchist.66
	title = rw_ger_monarchist.66.t
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_monarchist.66.d
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = GER_democracy_in_prussia
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_monarchist.66.d_2
	}
	picture = germany_election_monarchist

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #USPD
		name = rw_ger_monarchist.66.o1
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_monarchist_chancellor
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_monarchist_chancellor
						option = GER_MONARCHIST_CHANCELLOR_USPD
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_monarchist_chancellor
						option = GER_MONARCHIST_CHANCELLOR_KAMARILLA
					}					
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}		
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = GER_uspd_legalized
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = GER_westminister_democracy }
			}
			set_country_flag = GER_uspd_temp_victory_flag
			country_event = rw_ger_monarchist.71
		}
		else = {
			GER_set_ruling_party_monarchist_usdp = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { #Next Election
					id = rw_ger_monarchist.72
					days = 1463
				}
				country_event = { #SPD Leadership
					id = rw_ger_monarchist.68

			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_monarchist_chancellor

					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_monarchist_chancellor

					}					
				}
				factor = 0

country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_monarchist.73
	title = rw_ger_monarchist.73.t
	desc = rw_ger_monarchist.73.d
	picture = legalize_the_socialists

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #Yes
		name = rw_ger_monarchist.73.o1	
		set_country_flag = GER_uspd_legalized
		set_party_name = {
			name = GER_independent_social_democratic_party
			long_name = GER_independent_social_democratic_party_long
			ideology = moderate_socialist
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = moderate_socialist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
	}
	
	option = { #No
		name = rw_ger_monarchist.73.o2
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_monarchist_chancellor
						option = GER_MONARCHIST_CHANCELLOR_USPD
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_monarchist_chancellor
						option = GER_MONARCHIST_CHANCELLOR_KAMARILLA
					}					
				}	
			factor = 0
			}
		}		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = moderate_socialist
			popularity = -0.03
		}
	}
}

			NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_purged_all_commies }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_kaiser_is_hos }
			}
			GER_olaf_scholz = {
				promote_character = moderate_socialist_ideology
				set_portraits = {
					civilian = "gfx/leaders/GER/Portrait_GER_Olaf_Scholz_Sellout.png"
				}
				add_trait = {
					trait = GER_sacrificed_on_the_altar_of_neoliberalism
					ideology = moderate_socialist_ideology 
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_scholzomat_lives
		set_country_flag = GER_uspd_leader_scholz
		clr_country_flag = GER_uspd_leader_pellmann
		clr_country_flag = GER_uspd_leader_riexinger
	}
	
	option = { #Current person
		name = rw_ger_monarchist.77.o4
		
	}
}

	title = rw_ger_monarchist_diplo.55.t
	desc = rw_ger_monarchist_diplo.55.d
	picture = new_foreign_policy_angle

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { 
			has_completed_focus = GER_recapture_austria
			has_completed_focus = GER_reassert_polish_claims
			has_country_flag = GER_reclaiming_former_colonies
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Democratic Forpol
		name = rw_ger_monarchist_diplo.55.o1
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_monarchist_forpol
						option = GER_MONARCHIST_FORPOL_IMPERIALIST
					}
				}	
			factor = 0
			}
		}		
		unlock_national_focus = GER_democratic_foreign_policy
		set_country_flag = GER_monarchist_dem_forpol
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_dem_fp_warning_tt
		set_country_flag = GER_show_democratic_forpol_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
	
	option = { #Nah
		name = rw_ger_monarchist_diplo.55.o2
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_monarchist_forpol
						option = GER_MONARCHIST_FORPOL_IMPERIALIST
					}
				}	
			factor = 0
			}
		}		
		add_war_support = 0.04
	}
}

#Leaving the Warsaw Pact
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_democratic_diplo.1
	title = rw_ger_democratic_diplo.1.t
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_democratic_diplo.1.d_2
		trigger = { has_global_flag = FRA_is_faction_leader }
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_democratic_diplo.1.d
		trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = FRA_is_faction_leader } }
	}
	picture = germany_leaving_the_eu

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = { #
		name = rw_ger_democratic_diplo.1.o1
		if = {
			limit = { FRA = { is_faction_leader = yes } }
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = FRA }
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					modifier = betrayed_communism
					target = GER
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = SOV }
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					modifier = betrayed_communism
					target = GER
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ITA = { is_in_faction_with = FRA } }
			ITA = {
				country_event = rw_ger_democratic_diplo.2
			}
		}
		FRA = {
			country_event = rw_ger_democratic_diplo.2
		}
		BEL = {
			country_event = rw_ger_democratic_diplo.2
		}
		LUX = {
			country_event = rw_ger_democratic_diplo.2
		}
		HOL = {
			country_event = rw_ger_democratic_diplo.2
		}
	}
}

						}

							ruling_party = nationalist
						}
					}

						add_popularity = {
							ideology = national_conservative
							popularity = 0.2
						}
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = national_conservative
						}
					}
					20 = {
						add_popularity = {

						}

							ruling_party = centrist
						}

							popularity = 0.2

							ruling_party = liberal
						}
					}

							popularity = 0.2
						}

        set_country_flag = uniting_the_eu

			every_country = {
		        limit = {
			        NOT = {
				        tag = GER
				    }
			    }
			    news_event = {
			        hours = 2
			        id = news.205
		        }
		    }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_country_flag = uniting_the_eu }
				has_idea = idea_eu_member
			}
			country_event = rw_ger_european_union.38
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = EUU
		hidden_effect = {
		    remove_ideas = idea_ita_loyal_financial_institutions
			remove_ideas = idea_ita_euro
			remove_ideas = idea_ita_italian_president
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = SOV
			}
			remove_ideas = idea_comecon_member
		}
		SOV = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = GER
				modifier = rival
			}
		}
		GER = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = rival
			}
		}
	}
}

					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_communist_forpol
						option = DEFAULT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = GER_communist_forpol
						option = GER_COMMUNIST_FORPOL_WARSAW_CONFERENCE_WAR
					}						
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = {
				id = rw_ger_diplo.8
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

#EU-USSR Divorce who do we side with
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_diplo.12
	title = rw_ger_diplo.12.t
	desc = rw_ger_diplo.12.d
	picture = germany_euro_soviet_split
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {   #Side with Berlin
		name = rw_ger_diplo.12.o1
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				GER_is_great_european_war_pro_berlin = yes
				GER_is_great_european_war_neutral = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				check_variable = { GER_euroskeptic_fight > 2 }
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = GER_stood_with_us
			target = GER
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = GER_betrayed_us
			target = SOV
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_sided_with_the_ddr
		GER = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
	}
	
	option = {   #Side with Moscow
		name = rw_ger_diplo.12.o2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				GER_is_great_european_war_pro_moscow = yes
				GER_is_great_european_war_neutral = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = GER_stood_with_us
			target = SOV
		}
		
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = GER_betrayed_us
			target = GER
		}
		remove_ideas = idea_eu_member
		set_country_flag = SOV_sided_with_the_soviets
	}
	
	#FOR NON-STARTING TAGS
	
	option = {   #Side with Berlin
		name = rw_ger_diplo.12.o1
		trigger = {
			GER_is_great_european_war_pro_berlin = no
			GER_is_great_european_war_pro_moscow = no
			GER_is_great_european_war_neutral = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 20
				check_variable = { GER_euroskeptic_fight > 2 }
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = GER_stood_with_us
			target = GER
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = GER_betrayed_us
			target = SOV
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_sided_with_the_ddr
		GER = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
	}
	
	option = {   #Side with Moscow
		name = rw_ger_diplo.12.o2
		trigger = {
			GER_is_great_european_war_pro_berlin = no
			GER_is_great_european_war_pro_moscow = no
			GER_is_great_european_war_neutral = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = GER_stood_with_us
			target = SOV
		}
		
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			modifier = GER_betrayed_us
			target = GER
		}
		remove_ideas = idea_eu_member
		set_country_flag = SOV_sided_with_the_soviets
	}
}

#Germany - USSR sues for peace
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_diplo.17
	title = rw_ger_diplo.17.t
	desc = rw_ger_diplo.17.d
	picture = germany_ussr_surrenders
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {   #Give up
		name = rw_ger_diplo.17.o1
		set_country_flag = GER_beat_the_russians
		white_peace = SOV
		every_country = {
			limit = { 
				is_in_faction_with = SOV 
				NOT = { tag = SOV }
			}
			separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			SOV = { remove_from_faction = PREV }
			GER = { add_to_faction = PREV }
		}
		set_faction_name = warsaw_pact
		SOV = {
			separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			dismantle_faction = yes
			country_event = {
				id = rw_ger_diplo.22
				days = 5
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER  }
				has_country_flag = GER_sided_with_the_ddr
			}
			GER = { add_to_faction = PREV }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER  }
				has_country_flag = SOV_sided_with_the_soviets
			}
			GER = { add_to_faction = PREV }
		}
		GER_set_puppet_leaders = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = CAN_intervention_in_europe }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = CAN_sided_with_soviets }
				CAN = {
					country_event = {
						id = rw_ger_diplo.27
						days = 2
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				CAN = {
					country_event = {
						id = rw_ger_diplo.24
						days = 2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#USSR - Germans capture western SSRs
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_diplo.20
	title = rw_ger_diplo.20.t
	desc = rw_ger_diplo.20.d
	picture = germany_western_ssr_captured
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = SOV
		has_global_flag = GER_war_with_the_soviets
		has_country_flag = SOV_rejected_peace
		has_war_with = GER
		219 = {
			controller = {
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {   #Give up
		name = rw_ger_diplo.18.o1
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_political_power = -300
		GER = {
			country_event = rw_ger_diplo.21
		}
	}
}

#Germany - USSR sues for peace
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_diplo.21
	title = rw_ger_diplo.21.t
	desc = rw_ger_diplo.21.d
	picture = germany_ussr_surrenders
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {   #Give up
		name = rw_ger_diplo.21.o1
		set_country_flag = GER_beat_the_russians
		white_peace = SOV
		every_country = {
			limit = { 
				is_in_faction_with = SOV 
				NOT = { tag = SOV }
			}
			separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			SOV = { remove_from_faction = PREV }
			GER = { add_to_faction = PREV }
		}
		set_faction_name = warsaw_pact
		SOV = {
			separate_peace_all_wars = yes
			dismantle_faction = yes
			country_event = {
				id = rw_ger_diplo.22
				days = 5
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER  }
				has_country_flag = GER_sided_with_the_ddr
			}
			GER = { add_to_faction = PREV }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { 
				NOT = { is_in_faction_with = GER  }
				has_country_flag = SOV_sided_with_the_soviets
			}
			GER = { add_to_faction = PREV }
		}
		GER_set_puppet_leaders = yes
		GER_create_europakommisarat_ost = yes
		set_global_flag = SOV_lost_western_ssrs
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = CAN_intervention_in_europe }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = CAN_sided_with_soviets }
				CAN = {
					country_event = {
						id = rw_ger_diplo.27
						days = 2
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				CAN = {
					country_event = {
						id = rw_ger_diplo.24
						days = 2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

}

#Canada informed that war is over
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_diplo.24
	title = rw_ger_diplo.24.t
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_diplo.24.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = CAN_sided_with_soviets }
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = rw_ger_diplo.24.d_2
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = CAN_sided_with_soviets
		}
	}
	picture = germany_war_in_europe_over
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {   #Cool
		name = rw_ger_diplo.24.o1
		trigger = { has_global_flag = CAN_sided_with_soviets }
		white_peace = SOV
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = CAN_the_final_battle }
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = SOV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {   #Cool
		name = rw_ger_diplo.24.o1
		trigger = { NOT = { has_global_flag = CAN_sided_with_soviets } }
		white_peace = GER
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = CAN_the_final_battle }
			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = GER
			}
		}
	}
}

		transfer_state = 63
		transfer_state = 66
		transfer_state = 67
		add_state_claim = 743
		add_state_claim = 742
		add_state_claim = 63
		add_state_claim = 66
		add_state_claim = 67
	}

		name = rw_ger_diplo.25.o2

		add_stability = 0.02
	}
}

#SOV - Victory in Europe
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_diplo.26
	title = rw_ger_diplo.26.t
	desc = rw_ger_diplo.26.d
	picture = germany_soviet_victory
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		has_global_flag = GER_war_with_the_soviets
		has_war = no
		GER = { is_subject_of = SOV }
	}
	
	option = {   #Long live our Soviet Motherland!
		name = rw_ger_diplo.26.o1
		add_war_support = 0.05
		SOV_set_puppet_leaders = yes
		SOV_dissolve_germany = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = CAN_intervention_in_europe }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = CAN_sided_with_soviets }
				CAN = {
					country_event = {
						id = rw_ger_diplo.24
						days = 2
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				CAN = {
					country_event = {
						id = rw_ger_diplo.27
						days = 2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Czech Fate
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_diplo.32
	title = rw_ger_diplo.32.t
	desc = rw_ger_diplo.32.d
	picture = germany_divide_czechoslovakia
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {   #Divide
		name = rw_ger_diplo.32.o1
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = SLO }
			SLO = { transfer_state = PREV }
			remove_core_of = CZE
		}
		SLO_maros_sefcovic = {
			set_nationality = SLO
		}
		puppet = SLO
		SLO = {
			SLO_maros_sefcovic = {
				promote_character = leninist
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						expire = "1.1.1.1"
						ideology = leninist
					}
				}
				promote_character = leninist
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_government = communist }
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communist
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communist
					popularity = 0.45
				}
			}
			add_ideas = idea_eu_member
		}
		CZE = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = CZE_REP
		}
	}
	
	option = {   #Take
		name = rw_ger_diplo.32.o2
		every_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = SLO }
			SLO = { transfer_state = PREV }
			remove_core_of = CZE
		}
		SLO_maros_sefcovic = {
			set_nationality = SLO
		}
		puppet = SLO
		SLO = {
			SLO_maros_sefcovic = {
				promote_character = leninist
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						expire = "1.1.1.1"
						ideology = leninist
					}
				}
				promote_character = leninist
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_government = communist }
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communist
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = communist
					popularity = 0.45
				}
			}
			add_ideas = idea_eu_member
		}
		transfer_state = 69
		add_state_claim = 69
		CZE = { remove_state_core = 69 }
		CZE = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = CZE_REP
		}
	}
	
	option = {   #None
		name = rw_ger_diplo.32.o3
		custom_effect_tooltip = "No harm, no foul."
	}
}

	}

#Join the Warsaw Pact?
country_event = {
	id = rw_ger_diplo.35
	title = rw_ger_diplo.35.t
	desc = rw_ger_diplo.35.d
	picture = germany_join_warsaw_pact
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {   #Sure
		name = rw_ger_diplo.35.o1
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		GER = {
			add_to_faction = ROOT
			country_event = rw_ger_diplo.36
		}
	}
	
	option = {   #Nah
		name = rw_ger_diplo.35.o2
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_government = revolutionary_socialist
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = rw_ger_diplo.37
		}
	}
}

#GER - Post-USSR Country Joins the Warsaw Pact

	desc = rw_ger_diplo.36.d
	picture = germany_post_ussr_joins

			}

			}

				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rw_germany_flavour.63
				days = 4
			}
		}
	}
}
